    <script type="text/javascript">
        $(document).ready(function () {
            SetCookie('SWScreenWidth', screen.width);
            SetCookie('SWClientWidth', document.body.clientWidth);
            
            $("div.ui-article:last").addClass("last-article");
            $("div.region .app:last").addClass("last-app");

            // get on screen alerts
            var isAnyActiveOSA = 'False';
            var onscreenAlertCookie = GetCookie('Alerts');

            if (onscreenAlertCookie == '' || onscreenAlertCookie == undefined) {
                onscreenAlertCookie = "";
            }
            if (isAnyActiveOSA == 'True') {
                GetContent(homeURL + "/cms/Tools/OnScreenAlerts/UserControls/OnScreenAlertDialogListWrapper.aspx?OnScreenAlertCookie=" + onscreenAlertCookie + "&SiteID=4", "onscreenalert-holder", 2, "OnScreenAlertCheckListItem();");
            }

            

        });

    // ADA SKIP NAV
    $(document).ready(function () {
        $(document).on('focus', '#skipLink', function () {
            $("div.sw-skipnav-outerbar").animate({
                marginTop: "0px"
            }, 500);
        });

        $(document).on('blur', '#skipLink', function () {
            $("div.sw-skipnav-outerbar").animate({
                marginTop: "-30px"
            }, 500);
        });
    });

    // ADA MYSTART
    $(document).ready(function () {
        var top_level_nav = $('.sw-mystart-nav');

        // Set tabIndex to -1 so that top_level_links can't receive focus until menu is open
        // school dropdown
        $(top_level_nav).find('ul').find('a').attr('tabIndex', -1);

        // my account dropdown
        $(top_level_nav).next('ul').find('a').attr('tabIndex', -1);

        var openNavCallback = function(e, element) {
             // hide open menus
            hideMyStartBarMenu();

            // show school dropdown
            if ($(element).find('ul').length > 0) {
                $(element).find('.sw-dropdown').css('display', 'block').attr('aria-hidden', 'false');
                $(element).find('.sw-dropdown').find('li:first-child a').focus()
            }

            // show my account dropdown
            if ($(element).next('ul').length > 0) {
                $(element).next('.sw-dropdown').css('display', 'block').attr('aria-hidden', 'false');
                $(element).next('.sw-dropdown').find('li:first-child a').focus();
                $('#sw-mystart-account').addClass("clicked-state");
            }
        }

        $(top_level_nav).click(function (e) {
            openNavCallback(e, this);
        });

        $('.sw-dropdown-list li').click(function(e) {
            e.stopImmediatePropagation();
            $(this).focus();
        });
        
        // Bind arrow keys for navigation
        $(top_level_nav).keydown(function (e) {
            if (e.keyCode == 37) { //key left
                e.preventDefault();

                // This is the first item
                if ($(this).prev('.sw-mystart-nav').length == 0) {
                    $(this).parents('div').find('.sw-mystart-nav').last().focus();
                } else {
                    $(this).prev('.sw-mystart-nav').focus();
                }
            } else if (e.keyCode == 38) { //key up
                e.preventDefault();

                // show school dropdown
                if ($(this).find('ul').length > 0) {
                    $(this).find('div.sw-dropdown').css('display', 'block').find('ul').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').find('a').attr('tabIndex', 0).last().focus();
                }

                // show my account dropdown
                if ($(this).find('ul').length > 0) {
                    $(this).find('ul.sw-dropdown').css('display', 'block').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').find('a').attr('tabIndex', 0).last().focus();
                }
            } else if (e.keyCode == 39) { //key right
                e.preventDefault();

                // This is the last item
                if ($(this).next('.sw-mystart-nav').length == 0) {
                    $(this).parents('div').find('.sw-mystart-nav').first().focus();
                } else {
                    $(this).next('.sw-mystart-nav').focus();
                }
            } else if (e.keyCode == 40) { //key down
                e.preventDefault();

                // show school dropdown
                if ($(this).find('ul').length > 0) {
                    $(this).find('div.sw-dropdown').css('display', 'block').find('ul').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').find('a').attr('tabIndex', 0).first().focus();
                }

                // show my account dropdown
                if ($(this).next('ul').length > 0) {
                    $(this).next('ul.sw-dropdown').css('display', 'block').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').find('a').attr('tabIndex', 0).first().focus();
                }
            } else if (e.keyCode == 13 || e.keyCode == 32) { //enter key
                // If submenu is hidden, open it
                e.preventDefault();

                
                openNavCallback(e, this);
                $(this).parent('li').find('ul[aria-hidden=true]').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').find('a').attr('tabIndex', 0).first().focus();
            } else if (e.keyCode == 27) { //escape key
                e.preventDefault();
                hideMyStartBarMenu();
            } else {
                $(this).parent('.sw-mystart-nav').find('ul[aria-hidden=false] a').each(function () {
                    if (typeof keyCodeMap != "undefined" && $(this).text().substring(0, 1).toLowerCase() == keyCodeMap[e.keyCode]) {
                        $(this).focus();
                        return false;
                    }
                });
            }
        });

        // school dropdown
        var startbarlinks = $(top_level_nav).find('ul').find('a');
        bindMyStartBarLinks(startbarlinks);

        // my account dropdown
        var myaccountlinks = $(top_level_nav).next('ul').find('a');
        bindMyStartBarLinks(myaccountlinks);

        function bindMyStartBarLinks(links) {
            $(links).keydown(function (e) {
                e.stopPropagation();

                if (e.keyCode == 38) { //key up
                    e.preventDefault();

                    // This is the first item
                    if ($(this).parent('li').prev('li').length == 0) {
                        if ($(this).parents('ul').parents('.sw-mystart-nav').length > 0) {
                            $(this).parents('ul').parents('.sw-mystart-nav').focus();
                        } else {
                            $(this).parents('ul').prev('.sw-mystart-nav').focus();
                        }
                    } else {
                        $(this).parent('li').prev('li').find('a').first().focus();
                    }
                } else if (e.keyCode == 40) { //key down
                    e.preventDefault();

                    if ($(this).parent('li').next('li').length == 0) {
                        if ($(this).parents('ul').parents('.sw-mystart-nav').length > 0) {
                            $(this).parents('ul').parents('.sw-mystart-nav').focus();
                        } else {
                            $(this).parents('ul').prev('.sw-mystart-nav').focus();
                        }
                    } else {
                        $(this).parent('li').next('li').find('a').first().attr('tabIndex', 0);
                        $(this).parent('li').next('li').find('a').first().focus();
                    }
                } else if (e.keyCode == 27 || e.keyCode == 37) { // escape key or key left
                    e.preventDefault();
                    hideMyStartBarMenu();
                } else if (e.keyCode == 32) { //enter key
                    e.preventDefault();
                    window.location = $(this).attr('href');
                } else {
                    var found = false;

                    $(this).parent('div').nextAll('li').find('a').each(function () {
                        if (typeof keyCodeMap != "undefined" && $(this).text().substring(0, 1).toLowerCase() == keyCodeMap[e.keyCode]) {
                            $(this).focus();
                            found = true;
                            return false;
                        }
                    });

                    if (!found) {
                        $(this).parent('div').prevAll('li').find('a').each(function () {
                            if (typeof keyCodeMap != "undefined" && $(this).text().substring(0, 1).toLowerCase() == keyCodeMap[e.keyCode]) {
                                $(this).focus();
                                return false;
                            }
                        });
                    }
                }
            });
        }
        
        // Hide menu if click or focus occurs outside of navigation
        $('#sw-mystart-inner').find('.sw-mystart-nav').last().keydown(function (e) {
            if (e.keyCode == 9) {
                // If the user tabs out of the navigation hide all menus
                hideMyStartBarMenu();
            }
        });

        /*$(document).click(function() { 
            hideMyStartBarMenu();
        });*/

        // try to capture as many custom MyStart bars as possible
        $('.sw-mystart-button').find('a').focus(function () {
            hideMyStartBarMenu();
        });

        $('#sw-mystart-inner').click(function (e) {
            e.stopPropagation();
        });

        $('ul.sw-dropdown-list').blur(function () {
            hideMyStartBarMenu();
        });

        $('#ui-btn-mypasskey').focus(function () {
            hideMyStartBarMenu();
        });

        $('#ui-btn-sitemanager').focus(function () {
            hideMyStartBarMenu();
        });

        $('#ui-btn-myview').focus(function () {
            hideMyStartBarMenu();
        });

        $('#ui-btn-signin').focus(function () {
            hideMyStartBarMenu();
        });

        $('#ui-btn-register').focus(function () {
            hideMyStartBarMenu();
        });

        // button click events
        $('div.sw-mystart-button.home a').keydown(function (e) {
            e.stopImmediatePropagation();

            if (e.keyCode == 13) {
                $(this).click();
            }
        });

        $('div.sw-mystart-button.pw a').keydown(function (e) {
            e.stopImmediatePropagation();

            if (e.keyCode == 13) {
                $(this).click();
            }
        });

        $('div.sw-mystart-button.manage a').keydown(function (e) {
            e.stopImmediatePropagation();

            if (e.keyCode == 13) {
                $(this).click();
            }
        });

        $('#sw-mystart-account').keydown(function (e) {
            e.stopImmediatePropagation();

            if (e.keyCode == 13) {
                $(this).addClass('clicked-state');
                $('#sw-myaccount-list').show();
            }
        });

        $('#sw-mystart-mypasskey a').keydown(function (e) {
            e.stopImmediatePropagation();

            if (e.keyCode == 13) {
                $(this).click();
            }
        });

        $('div.sw-mystart-button.signin a').keydown(function (e) {
            e.stopImmediatePropagation();

            if (e.keyCode == 13) {
                $(this).click();
            }
        });

        $('div.sw-mystart-button.register a').keydown(function (e) {
            e.stopImmediatePropagation();

            if (e.keyCode == 13) {
                $(this).click();
            }
        });
    });

    function hideMyStartBarMenu() {
        $('.sw-dropdown').attr('aria-hidden', 'true').css('display', 'none');
        $('#sw-mystart-account').removeClass("clicked-state");
    }

    // ADA CHANNEL NAV
    $(document).ready(function() {
        var channelCount;
        var channelIndex = 1;
        var settings = {
            menuHoverClass: 'hover'
        };

        // Add ARIA roles to menubar and menu items
        $('[id="channel-navigation"]').attr('role', 'menubar').find('li a').attr('role', 'menuitem').attr('tabindex', '0');

        var top_level_links = $('[id="channel-navigation"]').find('> li > a');
        channelCount = $(top_level_links).length;


        $(top_level_links).each(function() {
            $(this).attr('aria-posinset', channelIndex).attr('aria-setsize', channelCount);
            $(this).next('ul').attr({ 'aria-hidden': 'true', 'role': 'menu' });

            if ($(this).parent('li.sw-channel-item').children('ul').length > 0) {
                $(this).attr('aria-haspopup', 'true');
            }

            var sectionCount = $(this).next('ul').find('a').length;
            var sectionIndex = 1;
            $(this).next('ul').find('a').each(function() {
                $(this).attr('tabIndex', -1).attr('aria-posinset', sectionIndex).attr('aria-setsize', sectionCount);
                sectionIndex++;
            });
            channelIndex++;

        });

        $(top_level_links).focus(function () {
            //hide open menus
            hideChannelMenu();

            if ($(this).parent('li').find('ul').length > 0) {
                $(this).parent('li').addClass(settings.menuHoverClass).find('ul').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').css('display', 'block');
            }
        });

        // Bind arrow keys for navigation
        $(top_level_links).keydown(function (e) {
            if (e.keyCode == 37) { //key left
                e.preventDefault();

                // This is the first item
                if ($(this).parent('li').prev('li').length == 0) {
                    $(this).parents('ul').find('> li').last().find('a').first().focus();
                } else {
                    $(this).parent('li').prev('li').find('a').first().focus();
                }
            } else if (e.keyCode == 38) { //key up
                e.preventDefault();

                if ($(this).parent('li').find('ul').length > 0) {
                    $(this).parent('li').addClass(settings.menuHoverClass).find('ul').css('display', 'block').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').find('a').attr('tabIndex', 0).last().focus();
                }
            } else if (e.keyCode == 39) { //key right
                e.preventDefault();

                // This is the last item
                if ($(this).parent('li').next('li').length == 0) {
                    $(this).parents('ul').find('> li').first().find('a').first().focus();
                } else {
                    $(this).parent('li').next('li').find('a').first().focus();
                }
            } else if (e.keyCode == 40) { //key down
                e.preventDefault();

                if ($(this).parent('li').find('ul').length > 0) {
                    $(this).parent('li')
                         .addClass(settings.menuHoverClass)
                         .find('ul').css('display', 'block')
                         .attr('aria-hidden', 'false')
                         .find('a').attr('tabIndex', 0)
                         .first().focus();
                }
            } else if (e.keyCode == 13 || e.keyCode == 32) { //enter key
                // If submenu is hidden, open it
                e.preventDefault();

                $(this).parent('li').find('ul[aria-hidden=true]').attr('aria-hidden', 'false').addClass(settings.menuHoverClass).find('a').attr('tabIndex', 0).first().focus();
            } else if (e.keyCode == 27) { //escape key
                e.preventDefault();
                hideChannelMenu();
            } else {
                $(this).parent('li').find('ul[aria-hidden=false] a').each(function () {
                    if (typeof keyCodeMap != "undefined" && $(this).text().substring(0, 1).toLowerCase() == keyCodeMap[e.keyCode]) {
                        $(this).focus();
                        return false;
                    }
                });
            }
        });

        var links = $(top_level_links).parent('li').find('ul').find('a');

        $(links).keydown(function (e) {
            if (e.keyCode == 38) {
                e.preventDefault();

                // This is the first item
                if ($(this).parent('li').prev('li').length == 0) {
                    $(this).parents('ul').parents('li').find('a').first().focus();
                } else {
                    $(this).parent('li').prev('li').find('a').first().focus();
                }
            } else if (e.keyCode == 40) {
                e.preventDefault();

                if ($(this).parent('li').next('li').length == 0) {
                    $(this).parents('ul').parents('li').find('a').first().focus();
                } else {
                    $(this).parent('li').next('li').find('a').first().focus();
                }
            } else if (e.keyCode == 27 || e.keyCode == 37) {
                e.preventDefault();
                $(this).parents('ul').first().prev('a').focus().parents('ul').first().find('.' + settings.menuHoverClass).removeClass(settings.menuHoverClass);
            } else if (e.keyCode == 32) {
                e.preventDefault();
                window.location = $(this).attr('href');
            } else {
                var found = false;

                $(this).parent('li').nextAll('li').find('a').each(function () {
                    if (typeof keyCodeMap != "undefined" && $(this).text().substring(0, 1).toLowerCase() == keyCodeMap[e.keyCode]) {
                        $(this).focus();
                        found = true;
                        return false;
                    }
                });

                if (!found) {
                    $(this).parent('li').prevAll('li').find('a').each(function () {
                        if (typeof keyCodeMap != "undefined" && $(this).text().substring(0, 1).toLowerCase() == keyCodeMap[e.keyCode]) {
                            $(this).focus();
                            return false;
                        }
                    });
                }
            }
        });

        function hideChannelMenu() {
            $('li.sw-channel-item.' + settings.menuHoverClass).removeClass(settings.menuHoverClass).find('ul').attr('aria-hidden', 'true').css('display', 'none').find('a').attr('tabIndex', -1);
        }
        
        // Hide menu if click or focus occurs outside of navigation
        $('[id="channel-navigation"]').find('a').last().keydown(function (e) {
            if (e.keyCode == 9) {
                // If the user tabs out of the navigation hide all menus
                hideChannelMenu();
            }
        });

        $('[id="channel-navigation"]').find('a').first().keydown(function (e) {
            if (e.keyCode == 9) {
                // hide open MyStart Bar menus
                hideMyStartBarMenu();
            }
        });

        /*$(document).click(function() {
            hideChannelMenu();
        });*/

        $('[id="channel-navigation"]').click(function (e) {
            e.stopPropagation();
        });
    });

    $(document).ready(function() {
        $('input.required').each(function() {
            if ($('label[for="' + $(this).attr('id') + '"]').length > 0) {
                if ($('label[for="' + $(this).attr('id') + '"]').html().indexOf('recStar') < 0) {
                    $('label[for="' + $(this).attr('id') + '"]').prepend('<span class="recStar" aria-label="required item">*</span> ');
                }
            }
        });

        $(document).ajaxComplete(function() {
            $('input.required').each(function() {
                if ($('label[for="' + $(this).attr('id') + '"]').length > 0) {
                    if ($('label[for="' + $(this).attr('id') + '"]').html().indexOf('recStar') < 0) {
                        $('label[for="' + $(this).attr('id') + '"]').prepend('<span class="recStar" aria-label="required item">*</span> ');
                    }
                }
            });
        });
    });
    </script>

    function customRedirectURL(){
	    if(window.location.href == "https://www.sumnersd.org/site/default.aspx?PageType=3&DomainID=4&ModuleInstanceID=1134&ViewID=6446EE88-D30C-497E-9316-3F8874B3E108&RenderLoc=0&FlexDataID=10671&PageID=1"){window.location = "http://sumnersd.org/boundaries";}
    }

	function jsQueries(){
		var getWidth = jsBreakPoint();
		if (getWidth == 960) { // 960
			photoGallery();
			channelMod();
			parallaxScroll();
		} if (getWidth == 768) { // 768
			photoGallery();
			channelMod();
			parallaxScroll();
		} if (getWidth == 640) { // 640
			photoGallery();
		} if (getWidth == 480) { // 480
			photoGallery();
		} if (getWidth == 320) { // 320
			photoGallery();
		}
	}
	
	function photoGallery(){
		head.ready("mediaRotator", function(){
			if(!$("#sw-content-container4.region.ui-hp .rs-gallery-container").length){
			        // MULTIMEDIA ROTATOR
			        $("#sw-content-container4.ui-hp div.ui-widget.app.cs-rs-multimedia-rotator").csRsMultimediaRotator({
			                //"imageWidth"              : 1280,
			                //"imageHeight"             : 445,
			                "imageWidth"              : 1120,
			                "imageHeight"             : 389,
			                "appHeader"               : "no",
			                "titles"                  : "yes",
			                "captions"                : "yes",
			                "galleryOverlay"          : "no",
			                "linkedElement"           : ["image", "title"], // ["image", "title", "overlay", "all"]
			                "playPause"               : "no",
			                "mainControls"            : "no",
			                "contMoreLink"            : "no",
			                "contMoreLinkText"        : "Read More",
			                "descMoreLink"            : "yes",
			                "descMoreLinkText"        : "LEARN MORE",
			                "bullets"                 : "yes",
			                "bulletControls"          : "no",
			                "thumbnails"              : "no",
			                "thumbnailWidth"          : 122,
			                "thumbnailHeight"         : 53,
			                "thumbnailSlideDirection" : "horizontal", // horizontal or vertical
			                "hoverPause"              : "yes",
			                "autoRotate"              : "yes",
			                "fullScreenRotator"       : "no", // image dimensions work well at 1500x915
			                "fullScreenVideo"         : "yes",
			                "transitionType"          : "fade", // fade or slide
			                "transitionSpeed"         : 3,
			                "transitionDelay"         : 8,
			                "onImageLoad"             : function() { },
			                "allImagesLoaded"         : function() { },
			                "onThumbnailLoad"         : function() { },
			                "allThumbnailsLoaded"     : function() { },
			                "onTransitionStart"       : function() { },
			                "onTransitionEnd"         : function() { },
			                "watchVidClick"           : function() { },
			                "closeVidClick"           : function() { },
			                "allLoaded"               : function() {
			                		// WRAP DESCRIPTION TITLE AND CAPTION
						$("#hp-slideshow .rs-gallery-desc").wrap("<div class='rs-gallery-desc-outer'></div>").children().wrapAll("<div class='rs-gallery-desc-inner'></div>");
			                		$("#hp-slideshow .rs-gallery-images li").first().append("<div class='rs-gallery-desc-accent-outer hide320'><div class='rs-gallery-desc-accent'><div class='rs-gallery-desc-accent-inner'></div></div></div>");
			                }
			        });
			}
		});
	}
	
	function viewFullSite() {
		if(!$("#gb-page.myview").length) {
			head.ready("fullSite", function() {
				// HEAD CONTENT
				$("body").viewFullSite({
					"breakPoint"		: 1023, // SYSTEM BREAK POINTS - 1023, 767, 639, 479
					"buttonContainer"	: "body",
					"useDefaultCSS"		: "yes",
					"fixedPosition"		: "bottom" // IF USING DEFAULT STYLES - TOP, BOTTOM
				});
			});
		}
	}	
	
	function useChannelForSection(){
		//DOC use channel name for pagelistnavigation header if one is not present
		if(!$("div.sp.column.one .ui-widget-header h1").length > 0) {
			$("div.sp.column.one .ui-widget-header").append("<h1></h1>");
		}
        }
        
	function dynamicContent(){
		// ********** MYSTART ********** //
		//DOC move mystart buttons and dropdowns
		
			// SIGN IN LINK
			var signInHref = $(".sw-mystart-button.signin a").attr("href");
//			$(".gb-mystart-myview.nli").attr("href", signInHref);
		
		// BUILD ATTENDANCE DROPDOWN
		var line1Check = "true";
		var line1 = jQuery.trim("(253) 891-6000");
		var line2Check = "false";
		var line2 = jQuery.trim("");
		var line3Check = "true";
		var line3 = jQuery.trim("(253) 891-5797");
		if(line1Check == "true" || line2Check == "true") {
			var attDD = '<div class="gb-mystart-list"><ul>';
			
			if(line1Check == "true") {
				attDD += '<li>Office: ' + line1 + '</li>';
			}
			if(line2Check == "true") {
				attDD += '<li>Attendance Line: ' + line2 + '</li>';
			}
			if(line3Check == "true") {
				attDD += '<li>Fax Number: ' + line3 + '</li>';
			}
			
			attDD += '</ul></div>';
			$(".gb-global-icon.attendance").append(attDD);
			
			$(".gb-global-icon.attendance").click(function() {
				$(".gb-mystart-list", this).toggle();
			});
		}

		// BUILD TIMES DROPDOWN
		var line1CheckTime = "false";
		var line1Time = jQuery.trim("8:25 a.m. - 3:10 p.m.");
		var line2CheckTime = "false";
		var line2Time = jQuery.trim("11:40 a.m.");
		var line3CheckTime = "false";
		var line3Time = jQuery.trim("10:00 a.m. - 3:10 p.m.");
		var line4CheckTime = "true";
		var line4Time = jQuery.trim("7:00 a.m. - 4:30 p.m.");
		if(line1CheckTime == "true" || line2CheckTime == "true" || line3CheckTime == "true" || line4CheckTime == "true") {
			var attDDTime = '<div class="gb-mystart-list"><ul>';
			
			if(line1CheckTime == "true") {
				attDDTime += '<li>Student Day: ' + line1Time + '</li>';
			}
			if(line2CheckTime == "true") {
				attDDTime += '<li>Half-Day Early Dismissal: ' + line2Time + '</li>';
			}
			if(line3CheckTime == "true") {
				attDDTime += '<li>Wednesday Late Start: ' + line3Time + '</li>';
			}
			if(line4CheckTime == "true") {
				attDDTime += '<li>Office Hours: ' + line4Time + '</li>';
			}
			
			attDDTime += '</ul></div>';
			$(".gb-global-icon.time").append(attDDTime);
			
			$(".gb-global-icon.time").click(function() {
				$(".gb-mystart-list", this).toggle();
			});
		}




		// ********** HEADER ********** //
		//DOC add logo
		if("true" == "true") {
			var logoSrc = jQuery.trim("/cms/lib/WA01919505/Centricity/Template/GlobalAssets/images///Faces/default-man.jpg");
			var srcSplit = logoSrc.split("/");
			var srcSplitLen = srcSplit.length;
			if(logoSrc != "" && srcSplit[srcSplitLen - 1] != "default-man.jpg") {
                //SHS, custom circle link to IB
                if('sumnersd' == 'shs'){
    				$("#gb-logo").html('<a href="/sumnersd"><img src="' + logoSrc + '" alt="Sumner School District" usemap="#shs-ib" /><map name="shs-ib"><area shape="circle" href="https://sites.google.com/edtools.sumnersd.org/shsib" target="_blank" coords="30,20,26"></map></a>').removeClass("hidden");
                } else {
    				$("#gb-logo").html('<a href="/sumnersd"><img src="' + logoSrc + '" alt="Sumner School District" /></a>').removeClass("hidden");
                }
				$("#hp-content-shortcut-logo").html('<a href="/sumnersd"><img src="' + logoSrc + '" alt="Sumner School District" /></a>');
			} else {
				$("#gb-logo").html('<a href="/sumnersd"><img src="/cms/lib/WA01919505/Centricity/Template/8/logos/sumner-logo.png" alt="Sumner School District" /></a>').removeClass("hidden");
				$("#hp-content-shortcut-logo").html('<a href="/sumnersd"><img src="/cms/lib/WA01919505/Centricity/Template/8/logos/sumner-logo.png" alt="Sumner School District" /></a>');
			}
		}
		//DOC add sitename
		var siteNameOne = jQuery.trim("SUMNER");
		var siteNameTwo = jQuery.trim("SCHOOL DISTRICT");
		if((siteNameOne == "") && (siteNameTwo == "")) {
			var splitLen = 2;
			var siteName = "Sumner School District";
			siteName = siteName.split(" ");
			var siteNameLength = siteName.length;
			if(siteNameLength > 2){
				siteNameEnd = jQuery.trim(siteName.splice(-splitLen, siteName.length).toString().replace(/,/g, " "));
			} else {
				siteNameEnd = jQuery.trim(siteName.splice(-1, siteName.length).toString().replace(/,/g, " "));
			}
			siteNameBegin = jQuery.trim(siteName.toString().replace(/,/g, " "));
			$("#gb-sitename").append('<a href="/sumnersd"><h1>' + siteNameBegin + '</h1></a><a href="/sumnersd"><h2>' + siteNameEnd + '</h2></a>');
		} else if((siteNameOne != "") && (siteNameTwo == "")) {
			$("#gb-sitename").append('<a href="/sumnersd"><h1>' + siteNameOne + '</h1></a>');
		} else if((siteNameOne == "") && (siteNameTwo != "")) {
			$("#gb-sitename").append('<a href="/sumnersd"><h1>' + siteNameTwo + '</h1></a>');
		} else if((siteNameOne != "") && (siteNameTwo != "")) {
			$("#gb-sitename").append('<a href="/sumnersd"><h1>' + siteNameOne + '</h1></a><a href="/sumnersd"><h2>' + siteNameTwo + '</h2></a>');
		}
		
		// AJAX IN THE SEARCH BOX
		if($(".sp").length) {
			// SESSION BASED HTML5 WEB STORAGE
			// CHECK IF IT IS SUPPORTED BY THE USERS BROWSER
			if(typeof(Storage) !== "undefined"){ // IS SUPPORTED
				if(sessionStorage.getItem("searchShortcuts") === null) {
					$("#gb-search-shortcuts").load("/sumnersd #gb-search-shortcuts-inner", function() {
						$("#gb-search-shortcuts .ui-widget.app.siteshortcuts ul.site-shortcuts").append('<li class="search">Search this site...</li>');
		        				search();
		        				
		        				var searchShortcutsHTML = $("#gb-search-shortcuts").html();
						sessionStorage.setItem("searchShortcuts", JSON.stringify(searchShortcutsHTML));
					});
				} else {
					$("#gb-search-shortcuts").html(JSON.parse(sessionStorage.getItem("searchShortcuts")));
					search();
				}
			} else { // IS NOT SUPPORTED
				$("#gb-search-shortcuts").load("/sumnersd #gb-search-shortcuts-inner", function() {
					$("#gb-search-shortcuts .ui-widget.app.siteshortcuts ul.site-shortcuts").append('<li class="search">Search this site...</li>');
	        				search();
				});
			}
		} else {
        		$("#gb-search-shortcuts .ui-widget.app.siteshortcuts ul.site-shortcuts").append('<li class="search">Search this site...</li>');
        		search();
		}
		
		// ********** CHANNEL BAR ********** //
        //MAKE ALL MEGA MENU CHANNEL BAR ITEMS NOT CLICKABLE
        $('li.sw-channel-item.mega').children('a').attr('href', 'javaScript:void(0)'); //Added by Lyndsay - Case #00305321 - 06-08-2016
		//DOC add first class to first channel item
		$("li.sw-channel-item").first().addClass("first");
		//DOC add last class to last channel item
		$("li.sw-channel-item").last().addClass("last");
		
		// ********** BODY ********** //
		//DOC rename first breadcrumb
		$("li.ui-breadcrumb-first > a > span").text("Home");
		//DOC replace more-link text
		$("a.more-link span").text("More ");
		//DOC auto-focus username signin field
		$("#swsignin-txt-username").focus();
		//DOC center signed out message and signin button
        	if($("div.ui-spn > div > p > span").text() == "You have been signed out."){
        		$("div.ui-spn > div").css({"text-align" : "center", "padding" : "50px 0px 50px 0px"});
        		//DOC add signed out breadcrumb
        		$(".ui-breadcrumbs").append("<li class='ui-breadcrumb-last'>Signed Out</li>");
        	}
        	//DOC add sign in breadcrumb
        	if($("#swlogin").length){
        		$(".ui-breadcrumbs").append("<li class='ui-breadcrumb-last'>Sign In</li>");
        	}
        	//DOC add read full story button to each headline
        	$(".ui-widget.app.headlines").each(function(){
        		$(".ui-article", this).each(function(){
        			var headlineURL = $("h1 a", this).attr("href");
        			$(".ui-article-description", this).append('<div><a class="custom-read-more" href="' + headlineURL + '"></a></div>');
        		});
        	});
        	// SET TEXT FOR BODY SHORTCUTS
        	var s = 0;
        	var shortcutNums = ["Headlines", "Construction", "Events", "Strategic Plan", "Family Services", "From the Superintendent", "Stay Connected", "District Staff"];
        	var shortcutSchoolNums = ["News", "From the Principal", "Events", "Family Services", "Athletics", "Clubs & Activities", "Stay Connected", "School Staff"];
        	$("#hp-content .hp-content-region-outer.scroll-nav").each(function() {
        		var headerTxt = jQuery.trim($(".ui-widget.app:first .ui-widget-header h1", this).text());
        		if(headerTxt == "") {
        		        if(window.location.pathname == "/" || window.location.pathname == "/Page/1" || window.location.pathname == "/site/default.aspx?PageID=1" || window.location.pathname == "/sumnersd"){
        		           headerTxt = shortcutNums[s];
        		        } else {
        		           headerTxt = shortcutSchoolNums[s];
        		        }
        		}
        		
        		$(".hp-content-shortcut:eq(" + s + ") a span.text").text(headerTxt);
        		
        		s++;
        	});
        	// MODIFY CHANNEL ICON
        	if(window.location.pathname == "/lms"){
        		$(".hp-content-shortcut.sw-content-container10 > a > span.icon").css({'font-size': '32px'});
        	}
        	// BODY SHORTCUT CLICK
        	$(".hp-content-shortcut").click(function(e) {
        		e.preventDefault();
        		var channelBarH = $("#gb-channel-list").height();
        		var contentID = "sw-content-" + $("a", this).attr("id").replace("hp-region-", "");
        		var shortcutsH = $("#hp-content-shortcuts-outer").height() + (channelBarH + 48);
        		var docOffset = $("#" + contentID).offset().top - shortcutsH;
        		
        		$("html, body").animate({
				scrollTop: ($("#" + contentID).offset().top - shortcutsH) + 1
			}, 500, function(){
				$("html, body").stop(true, false);
				shortcutsH = $("#hp-content-shortcuts-outer").height() + (channelBarH + 48);
        			docOffset = $("#" + contentID).offset().top - shortcutsH;
				$(document).scrollTop(($("#" + contentID).offset().top - shortcutsH) + 1);
			});
        	});
        	// ADD CLASSES TO SITE SHORTCUTS
        	$("div.ui-widget.app.navigation.siteshortcuts").each(function() {
        		var linkNum = $("ul.site-shortcuts > li", this).length;
        		var linkClasses = ["one", "two", "three", "four"];
        		var c = 0;
        		for(var i = 0; i < linkNum; i++) {
        			$("ul.site-shortcuts > li", this).eq(i).addClass(linkClasses[c]);
        			
        			c++;
				if(c == 4) {
					c = 0;
				}
        		}
  		});
  		// HOMEPAGE EMPLOYEE PHOTO
  		//DOC add logo
		var staffImg = jQuery.trim("/cms/lib/WA01919505/Centricity/Template/GlobalAssets/images///SSD_template/district-employee-picture.png");
		var imgSplit = staffImg.split("/");
		var imgSplitLen = imgSplit.length;
		if(staffImg != "" && imgSplit[imgSplitLen - 1] != "default-man.jpg") {
			if("sumnersd" == district) {
				$(".hp-content-region-outer.container13").prepend('<img src="' + staffImg + '" alt="Our staff makes the difference" />');
				$(".hp-content-region-outer.container13 .hp-content-region").html('<div id="hp-employee-img-overlay">our staff makes the difference<a href="/Page/3656" class="call-to-action-white">STAFF DIRECTORY</a></div>');
			} else {
				$(".hp-content-region-outer.container13").prepend('<img src="' + staffImg + '" alt="Our staff make the difference" />');
				$(".hp-content-region-outer.container13 .hp-content-region").html('<div id="hp-employee-img-overlay">our staff make the difference<a href="/Page/3656" class="call-to-action-white">STAFF DIRECTORY</a></div>');
			}
		}
		// SCROLL TO TOP
		$("#gb-page-scroll a").click(function(e) {
			e.preventDefault();
			$("html, body").animate({ scrollTop: 0 }, "slow");
		});
		// CHECK AND SET GOOD TO KNOW QUICKLINKS APP
		if($(".sp.two").length) {
			if($(".sp.two #sw-content-layout-wrapper .ui-widget.app").last().hasClass("siteshortcuts")) {
				$(".sp.two #sw-content-layout-wrapper .ui-widget.app").last().addClass("cs-gtk-links");
			}
		}
		if($("#spn-content").length) {
			if($("#spn-content #sw-content-layout-wrapper .ui-widget.app").last().hasClass("siteshortcuts")) {
				$("#spn-content #sw-content-layout-wrapper .ui-widget.app").last().addClass("cs-gtk-links");
			}
		}
		// APPLY RESPONSIVE DIMENSIONS TO CONTENT IMAGES
        	$("div.ui-widget.app .ui-widget-detail img").not($("div.ui-widget.app.cs-rs-multimedia-rotator .ui-widget-detail img, .ui-widget.staffdirectorydiv.app .ui-widget-detail img")).each(function() {
			$(this).css({"display": "inline-block", "width": "100%", "max-width": $(this).attr("width") + "px", "height": "auto", "max-height": $(this).attr("height") + "px"});
		});
		// CHECK FOR APP SIDEBAR
		$(document).ajaxComplete(function() {
			if($(".ui-widget-sidebar").length) {
				$(".blog .ui-widget-sidebar, .headlines .ui-widget-sidebar").each(function() {
					$(this).parent().addClass("has-sidebar");
				});
			}
		});
		// MYVIEW SCHOOL DROPDOWN
		$("#gb-schools-btn a, .gb-school-link.close a").click(function(e) {
			e.preventDefault();
			if($("#gb-school-links").hasClass("closed")) {
				$("#gb-school-links").removeClass("closed hidden").addClass("open");
			} else {
				$("#gb-school-links").removeClass("open").addClass("closed hidden");
			}
		});
       	
		
		// ********** FOOTER ********** //
		//DOC get Schoolwires footer links
		$("a#feedback").text($("div#sw-footer-links li:eq(0) a").text()).attr("href", $("div#sw-footer-links li:eq(0) a").attr("href"));
		$("a#terms").text($("div#sw-footer-links li:eq(2) a").text()).attr("href", $("div#sw-footer-links li:eq(2) a").attr("href"));
		$("a#policy").text($("div#sw-footer-links li:eq(1) a").text().replace(" (Updated)", "")).attr("href", $("div#sw-footer-links li:eq(1) a").attr("href"));		
	}
	
	function dynamicStyleSheet() {
		var primaryColor8 = "rgba(" + hexToRgb("#b7b207") + ", 0.08)";
		var primaryColor10 = "rgba(" + hexToRgb("#b7b207") + ", 0.10)";
		var primaryColor15 = "rgba(" + hexToRgb("#b7b207") + ", 0.15)";
		var primaryColor30 = "rgba(" + hexToRgb("#b7b207") + ", 0.30)";
		var primaryColor80 = "rgba(" + hexToRgb("#b7b207") + ", 0.80)";
		var secondaryColor10 = "rgba(" + hexToRgb("#005595") + ", 0.10)";
		var secondaryColor50 = "rgba(" + hexToRgb("#005595") + ", 0.50)";
		var secondaryColor60 = "rgba(" + hexToRgb("#005595") + ", 0.60)";
		var secondaryColor80 = "rgba(" + hexToRgb("#005595") + ", 0.80)";
		var secondaryColor85 = "rgba(" + hexToRgb("#005595") + ", 0.85)";
		
		var dynStyleSheet = document.createElement('style');
		if(dynStyleSheet) {
			dynStyleSheet.setAttribute('type', 'text/css');
			var head = document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0];
			if(head) {
				head.insertBefore(dynStyleSheet, head.childNodes[0]);
			}
			
			var dynStyles =	".hp-content-shortcut a {" +
						"background: #b7b207;" +
						"background: " + primaryColor30 + ";" +
					"}" +
					"#view-full-site, " +
					"#rs-menu:before, " +
					".rs-menu-option .rs-menu-option-header, " +
					"#rs-menu-search, " +
					".rs-menu-option-sublist > li.rs-menu-option-sublist-header, " +
					".rs-menu-option-sublist:before {" +
						"background: " + secondaryColor80 + " !important;" +
					"}" +
					".rs-menu-channels .rs-menu-option-sublist .page-navigation {" +
						"background: " + secondaryColor10 + " !important;" +
					"}";
			var rules = document.createTextNode(dynStyles);
			if(dynStyleSheet.styleSheet){ // IE
				dynStyleSheet.styleSheet.cssText = dynStyles;
			} else {
				dynStyleSheet.appendChild(rules);
			}
		}
	}
	
	function hexToRgb(h){
	        var r = parseInt((cutHex(h)).substring(0,2),16);
	        var g = parseInt((cutHex(h)).substring(2,4),16);
	        var b = parseInt((cutHex(h)).substring(4,6),16);
	        return r + ', ' + g + ', ' + b;
	}
	 
	function cutHex(h) {
	        return (h.charAt(0)=="#") ? h.substring(1,7):h;
	}
	
	function custom404() {
		if($("div.ui-widget.error-404").length) {
			// SESSION BASED HTML5 WEB STORAGE
			// CHECK IF IT IS SUPPORTED BY THE USERS BROWSER
			if(typeof(Storage) !== "undefined"){ // IS SUPPORTED
				if(sessionStorage.getItem("custom404") === null) {
					// DO STUFF IF THE ITEM DOES NOT EXIST IN STORAGE
					$("div.ui-widget.error-404").empty().load("/page/1175 #sw-content-container1", function() {
						$(this).show();
						
						// THEN STORE WHAT YOU NEED
						// JSON STRINGIFY IS USED BECAUSE SOME JAVASCRIPT WILL BE STORED
						var stuffToStore = $("div.ui-widget.error-404").html();
						sessionStorage.setItem("custom404", JSON.stringify(stuffToStore));
					});
				} else {
					// DO STUFF IF THE ITEM DOES EXIST IN STORAGE
					// JSON PARSE IS USED BECAUSE OF THE CONTAINED JAVASCRIPT
					$("div.ui-widget.error-404").html(JSON.parse(sessionStorage.getItem("custom404"))).show();
				}
			} else { // IS NOT SUPPORTED
				$("div.ui-widget.error-404").empty().load("/page/1175 #sw-content-container1", function() {
					$(this).show();
				});
			}
		}
	}
	
	function spHeaderResize() {
		if($(".sp").length) {
			var headerH = $("#gb-page-top").height();
			// CHECK HEIGHT AGAINST GLOBAL VARIABLE SO WE ONLY HIT THE DOM WHEN WE HAVE TO
			if(headerH != spHeaderH) {
				$("#gb-page-bottom").css("padding-top", headerH + "px");
				spHeaderH = headerH;
			}
		}
	}

	function csEventsCalendar() {
		head.ready("eventsCalendar", function() {
			$(".hp .upcomingevents").eventsCalendar({
				"calendarLinkText"	: "View Full Calendar",
				"RSSLinkText"		: "Subscribe To This Calendar",
				"calLoad"		: function() {}
			});
		});
	}
	
	function contactForm() {
		// SELECT DROPDOWNS
		var schoolsList = formSchools.split(","), contactSchools = "";
		for(var s in schoolsList) {
			contactSchools += '<li>' + jQuery.trim(schoolsList[s]) + '</li>';
		}
		$(".gb-form-select.select-school .gb-form-select-dropdown ul").html(contactSchools);
		
		var reasonsList = formReasons.split(","), contactReasons = "";
		for(var r in reasonsList) {
			contactReasons += '<li>' + jQuery.trim(reasonsList[r]) + '</li>';
		}
		$(".gb-form-select.contact-reason .gb-form-select-dropdown ul").html(contactReasons);
		
		$(".gb-form-select").click(function() {
			if($(".gb-form-select-dropdown", this).hasClass("closed")) {
				$(".gb-form-select-dropdown", this).removeClass("closed").addClass("open");
			} else {
				$(".gb-form-select-dropdown", this).addClass("closed").removeClass("open");
			}
		});

		$(".gb-form-select-dropdown li").click(function() {
			var selectedVal = $.trim($(this).text());
			var dropdownParent = $(this).parents(".gb-form-select");
			
			$(".gb-form-select-val", dropdownParent).val(selectedVal);
			$(".gb-form-select-preview", dropdownParent).text(selectedVal);
		});
	
		// FOCUS AND BLUR EVENTS
		$("#gb-form-first-name").focus(function() {
			if($(this).val() == "First Name") {
				$(this).val("");
			}
		}).blur(function() {
			if($(this).val() == "") {
				$(this).val("First Name");
			}
		});
		$("#gb-form-last-name").focus(function() {
			if($(this).val() == "Last Name") {
				$(this).val("");
			}
		}).blur(function() {
			if($(this).val() == "") {
				$(this).val("Last Name");
			}
		});
		$("#gb-form-email").focus(function() {
			if($(this).val() == "Email Address") {
				$(this).val("");
			}
		}).blur(function() {
			if($(this).val() == "") {
				$(this).val("Email Address");
			}
		});
		$("#gb-form-phone").focus(function() {
			if($(this).val() == "Phone Number") {
				$(this).val("");
			}
		}).blur(function() {
			if($(this).val() == "") {
				$(this).val("Phone Number");
			}
		});
		
		// FORM IS SUBMITTED
		$("#gb-contact-form").submit(function(e) {
			e.preventDefault();
			// SET UP VARIABLES
			var error = 0, errMsgs = "", inputID = "", selectVal = "";
			var firstName = jQuery.trim($("#gb-form-first-name").val());
			var lastName = jQuery.trim($("#gb-form-last-name").val());
			var email = jQuery.trim($("#gb-form-email").val());
			var phone = jQuery.trim($("#gb-form-phone").val());
			var school = $("#gb-form-school").val();
			var contactReason = $("#gb-form-reason").val();
			
			// VALIDATE THE FORM
			$(".gb-form-col input[type=text]").each(function() {
				inputID = jQuery.trim($(this).attr("id").replace("gb-form-", ""));
				switch(inputID) {
					case "first-name" :
						if(jQuery.trim($(this).val()) == "First Name" ||  jQuery.trim($(this).val()) == "") {
							error = 1;
							errMsgs += "<p>Please enter your first name.</p>";
						}
					break;
					case "last-name" :
						if(jQuery.trim($(this).val()) == "Last Name" ||  jQuery.trim($(this).val()) == "") {
							error = 1;
							errMsgs += "<p>Please enter your last name.</p>";
						}
					break;
					case "email" :
						if(validateEmail(jQuery.trim($(this).val())) == false) {
							error = 1;
							errMsgs += "<p>Please enter a valid email address.</p>";
						}
					break;
					case "phone" :
						if(jQuery.trim($(this).val()) == "Phone Number" ||  jQuery.trim($(this).val()) == "") {
							error = 1;
							errMsgs += "<p>Please enter your phone number.</p>";
						}
					break;
				}
			});
			
			// SELECT DROPDOWN VALUES
			if($("#gb-form-school").val() == "") {
				error = 1;
				errMsgs += "<p>Please select a school.</p>";
			}
			
			if($("#gb-form-reason").val() == "") {
				error = 1;
				errMsgs += "<p>Please select a contact reason.</p>";
			}
			
			
			if(error == 0) {
				$("#gb-form-submit").val("Sending Mail...");
			
				// SEND THE MAIL	
				$.ajax({
					url : "//classicasp.schoolwires.net/twitter/Sumner_Email_Service/sendMail.asp?callback=?",
					dataType: "jsonp",
					contentType: "application/json; charset=utf-8",
					async: false,
					data : { "formRecipient": formRecipient, "domain": window.location.host, "firstName": firstName, "lastName": lastName, "email": email, "phone": phone, "school": school, "contactReason": contactReason },
					success: function(data) {
						if(data.msg == "success"){
							$("#gb-form-msgs").html("<p style='text-align: center;'>Your message has been sent!</p><p style='text-align: center;'>Thank you!</p>");
							$("#gb-form-window-outer").fadeIn("fast");
							
							// RESET THE FIELDS
							var fieldVals = ["First Name", "Last Name", "Email Address", "Phone Number"], i = 0;
							$(".gb-form-col input[type=text]").each(function() {
								$(this).val(fieldVals[i]);
								i++;
							});
							$("#gb-form-school").val("");
							$("#gb-form-reason").val("");
							$(".gb-form-select.select-school .gb-form-select-preview").text("Select a School");
							$(".gb-form-select.contact-reason .gb-form-select-preview").text("Select a Contact Reason");
							
							$("#gb-form-submit").val("SUBMIT");
						} else {
							$("#gb-form-msgs").html("<p>An error occured.</p><p>The error details are: " + data.err + "</p>");
							$("#gb-form-window-outer").fadeIn("fast");
							
							$("#gb-form-submit").val("SUBMIT");
						}
					}
				});
			} else {
				$("#gb-form-msgs").html(errMsgs);
				$("#gb-form-window-outer").fadeIn("fast");
			}
		});
		
		$("#gb-form-window-outer, #gb-form-window-close").click(function() {
			$("#gb-form-window-outer").fadeOut("fast", function() {
				$("#gb-form-msgs").empty();
			});
		});
		$("#gb-form-window").click(function() {
			return false;
		});
	}
	
	function calendarEvents() {
	   $( ".cs-has-events:first" ).trigger( "click" );
	}
	
	function validateEmail(email) {
		var eAddress = email;
		var atpos = eAddress.indexOf("@");
		var dotpos = eAddress.lastIndexOf(".");
		if (atpos < 1 || dotpos < atpos + 2 || dotpos + 2 >= eAddress.length) {
			return false;
		} else {
			return true;
		}
	}
	
	function parallaxScroll() {
		if($(".hp").length) {
			var channelBarH = $("#gb-channel-list").height();
			var getWidth = jsBreakPoint();
			if(getWidth == 960) {
				if($("body").height() >= 2000) {
					// STICKY CHANNEL BAR
					var channelBarOffset = $("#gb-channel-list-outer").offset().top;
					if (($(window).scrollTop() + 48) <= channelBarOffset) {
						if(channelBarIsSticky) {
							$("#gb-channel-list-inner").removeClass("sticky-channel-bar");
							$("#gb-channel-list-outer").css("height", "auto");
							
							channelBarIsSticky = 0;
						}
					} else {
						if(!channelBarIsSticky) {
							$("#gb-channel-list-inner").addClass("sticky-channel-bar");
							
							channelBarIsSticky = 1;
						}
						
						$("#gb-channel-list-outer").css("height", $("#gb-channel-list").height() + "px");
					}
				
					// GET THE TOP POSITION OF THE TABS CONTAINER
					var shortcutsPos = $("#gb-page-top").height();
					
					// USING THE stickyshortcuts VARIABLE TO AVOID HITTING THE DOM EVERY TIME A USER SCROLLS
					// THIS WAY WE ONLY MAKE CHANGES WHEN THEY ARE NEEDED
					
					if(($(window).scrollTop() + channelBarH) < shortcutsPos) {
						// IF stickyshortcuts NEEDS TURNED OFF
						if(stickyShortcuts == 0 || stickyShortcuts == 1) {
							$("#hp-content-shortcuts-outer").removeClass("sticky").css("top", "auto");
							$("#hp-content").css("padding-top", "0px");
							$(".hp-content-shortcut a span.text").slideDown(250);
							$("#hp-content-shortcuts-watermark").fadeIn(250);
							$("#hp-content-shortcuts").animate({
								"padding-top" : "80px",
								"padding-right" : "0px",
								"padding-bottom" : "55px",
								"padding-left" : "0px",
							}, 250);
							
							stickyShortcuts = 2;
						}
						
						if(activeShortcut != 0) {
							$(".hp-content-shortcut").removeClass("active");
							activeShortcut = 0;
						}
					} else {
						// IF NEEDS TURNED ON
						if(stickyShortcuts == 0 || stickyShortcuts == 2) {
							$(".hp-content-shortcut a span.text").slideUp(250);
							$("#hp-content-shortcuts-watermark").fadeOut(250);
							$("#hp-content-shortcuts").animate({
								"padding-top" : "8px",
								"padding-right" : "0px",
								"padding-bottom" : "8px",
								"padding-left" : "0px",
							}, 250, function() {
								
								$("#hp-content").css("padding-top", $("#hp-content-shortcuts-outer").height() + "px");
							});
							
							stickyShortcuts = 1;
						}
						$("#hp-content-shortcuts-outer").addClass("sticky").css("top", (channelBarH + 48) + "px");
						
						// SET THE ACTIVE SHORTCUT
						setShortcut($(window).scrollTop());
					}
					
					if(pScroll == 0) { pScroll = 1; }
				}
			} else if (getWidth <= 768) {
				if(pScroll == 1) {
					$("#hp-content-shortcuts-outer").removeClass("sticky").css("top", "auto");
					$("#hp-content").css("padding-top", "0px");
					$(".hp-content-shortcut a span.text").show();
					$("#hp-content-shortcuts-watermark").show();
					$("#hp-content-shortcuts").css("padding", "80px 0px 55px");
					$("#gb-channel-list-outer").removeClass("sticky-header").css("height", "auto");
					$("#gb-channel-list-inner").removeClass("sticky-channel-bar");
					
					channelBarIsSticky = 0;
					stickyShortcuts = 2;
					pScroll = 0;
				}
			}
		} else {
			if($(window).scrollTop() > 0) {
				if(spParallax == 0) {
					$(".sp #gb-channel-list-outer").addClass("scrolling");
					spParallax = 1;
				}
			} else {
				if(spParallax == 1) {
					$(".sp #gb-channel-list-outer").removeClass("scrolling");
					spParallax = 0;
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	function parallaxScrollReset(){
		if($(".hp").length) {
			$("#gb-channel-list-outer").removeClass("sticky-header").css("height", "auto");
			$("#gb-channel-list-inner").removeClass("sticky-channel-bar");
			$("#hp-content-shortcuts-outer").removeClass("sticky").css("top", "auto");
			$("#gb-page-bottom").css("padding-top", "0px");
		}
	}
	
	function setShortcut(scrollPos) {
		if($(".hp").length) {
			// USING THE activeShortcut VARIABLE TO AVOID HITTING THE DOM EVERY TIME A USER SCROLLS
			// THIS WAY WE ONLY MAKE CHANGES WHEN THEY ARE NEEDED
			var channelBarH = $("#gb-channel-list").height();
			var shortcutsH = $("#hp-content-shortcuts-outer").height() + (channelBarH + 48);
			var container5Pos = $("#sw-content-container5.ui-hp").offset().top - shortcutsH;
			var container6Pos = $("#sw-content-container6.ui-hp").offset().top - shortcutsH;
			var container7Pos = $("#sw-content-container7.ui-hp").offset().top - shortcutsH;
			var container8Pos = $("#sw-content-container8.ui-hp").offset().top - shortcutsH;
			var container9Pos = $("#sw-content-container9.ui-hp").offset().top - shortcutsH;
			var container10Pos = $("#sw-content-container10.ui-hp").offset().top - shortcutsH;
			var container11Pos = $("#sw-content-container11.ui-hp").offset().top - shortcutsH;
			var container12Pos = $("#sw-content-container12.ui-hp").offset().top - shortcutsH;
			
			if(scrollPos >= container5Pos && scrollPos < container6Pos) {
				if(activeShortcut != 1) {
					$(".hp-content-shortcut").removeClass("active");
					$(".hp-content-shortcut.sw-content-container5").addClass("active");
					activeShortcut = 1;
				}
			} 
			if(scrollPos >= container6Pos && scrollPos < container7Pos) {
				if(activeShortcut != 2) {
					$(".hp-content-shortcut").removeClass("active");
					$(".hp-content-shortcut.sw-content-container6").addClass("active");
					activeShortcut = 2;
				}
			}
			if(scrollPos >= container7Pos && scrollPos < container8Pos) {
				if(activeShortcut != 3) {
					$(".hp-content-shortcut").removeClass("active");
					$(".hp-content-shortcut.sw-content-container7").addClass("active");
					activeShortcut = 3;
				}
			}
			if(scrollPos >= container8Pos && scrollPos < container9Pos) {
				if(activeShortcut != 4) {
					$(".hp-content-shortcut").removeClass("active");
					$(".hp-content-shortcut.sw-content-container8").addClass("active");
					activeShortcut = 4;
				}
			}
			if(scrollPos >= container9Pos && scrollPos < container10Pos) {
				if(activeShortcut != 5) {
					$(".hp-content-shortcut").removeClass("active");
					$(".hp-content-shortcut.sw-content-container9").addClass("active");
					activeShortcut = 5;
				}
			}
			if(scrollPos >= container10Pos && scrollPos < container11Pos) {
				if(activeShortcut != 6) {
					$(".hp-content-shortcut").removeClass("active");
					$(".hp-content-shortcut.sw-content-container10").addClass("active");
					activeShortcut = 6;
				}
			}
			if(scrollPos >= container11Pos && scrollPos < container12Pos) {
				if(activeShortcut != 7) {
					$(".hp-content-shortcut").removeClass("active");
					$(".hp-content-shortcut.sw-content-container11").addClass("active");
					activeShortcut = 7;
				}
			}
			if(scrollPos >= container12Pos) {
				if(activeShortcut != 8) {
					$(".hp-content-shortcut").removeClass("active");
					$(".hp-content-shortcut.sw-content-container12").addClass("active");
					activeShortcut = 8;
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	function channelMod() {
	        // RESET THE MARGIN
	        $("li.sw-channel-item").css("margin", "");
	               
	        // SET UP OUR VARIABLES
	        var channelNum = $("li.sw-channel-item").length, channelWidths = 0, channelBarWidth = $("#sw-channel-list-container").width() - 1, availSpace = 0, channelPad = 0;
	               
	        // GET THE TOTAL WIDTH OF ALL THE CHANNELS
	        $("li.sw-channel-item").each(function(){
	                channelWidths += $(this).width();
	        });
	               
	        // GET THE TOTAL AMOUNT OF EMPTY SPACE LEFT OVER
	        availSpace = channelBarWidth - channelWidths;
	               
	        // GET THE AMOUNT OF SPACE TO SET BETWEEN EACH CHANNEL
	        // SUBTRACT ONE FROM THE TOTAL CHANNEL NUMBER BECAUSE WE WANT THE LAST CHANNEL TO SIT AGAINST THE RIGHT EDGE OF THE TEMPLATE
	        channelPad = Math.floor(availSpace / (channelNum - 1));
	               
	        // NOW APPLY THE MARGIN
	        $("li.sw-channel-item").not($("li.sw-channel-item.last")).css("margin-right", channelPad + "px");
	        
	        // ADD DIMENSIONS FOR HOVER AND ACTIVE BACKGROUNDS
	        var activeStyles = 	"<style type='text/css'>" +
	        					"li.sw-channel-item.hover > a:before, li.sw-channel-item.active > a:before, .ie8 li.sw-channel-item.hover > a > .before, .ie8 li.sw-channel-item.active > a > .before {" +
	        						"left: -" + (Math.floor(channelPad / 2)) + "px;" +
	        						"right: -" + (Math.floor(channelPad / 2)) + "px;" +
	        					"}" +
	        				"</style>";
		if(channelStyles == 0) {
			$("#sw-channel-list-container").append("<div id='gb-channel-active-styles'>" + activeStyles + "</div>");
			channelStyles = 1;
		} else {
			$("#gb-channel-active-styles").html(activeStyles);
		}
	        
	}

	function search() {
		// DROPDOWN ARROW CLICK
		/*
		$(".gb-search-btn.dropdown").click(function() {
			if($(this).hasClass("closed")) {
				$(this).removeClass("closed").addClass("open")
				$("#gb-search-shortcuts").removeClass("closed").addClass("open").show();
			} else {
				$(this).removeClass("open").addClass("closed")
				$("#gb-search-shortcuts").removeClass("open").addClass("closed").hide();
			}
		});
		$("#gb-search-inner").not($(".gb-search-btn.search")).hover(function() {
			$(".gb-search-btn.dropdown").removeClass("closed").addClass("open")
			$("#gb-search-shortcuts").removeClass("closed").addClass("open").show();
		}, function () {
			$(".gb-search-btn.dropdown").removeClass("open").addClass("closed")
			$("#gb-search-shortcuts").removeClass("open").addClass("closed").hide();
		});
		
		// SEARCH WINDOW CLICK
		$("#gb-search-window").click(function() {
			if($(".gb-search-btn.dropdown").hasClass("closed")) {
				$(".gb-search-btn.dropdown").removeClass("closed").addClass("open")
				$("#gb-search-shortcuts").removeClass("closed").addClass("open").show();
			} else {
				$(".gb-search-btn.dropdown").removeClass("open").addClass("closed")
				$("#gb-search-shortcuts").removeClass("open").addClass("closed").hide();
			}
		});
		
		// DISABLE TO SHORTCUT CLICK DEFAULT
		$("#gb-search-shortcuts .ui-widget.app.siteshortcuts ul.site-shortcuts li a").click(function(e) {
			e.preventDefault();
			// CLOSE EVERYTHING UP
			$(".gb-search-btn.dropdown").removeClass("open").addClass("closed")
			$("#gb-search-shortcuts").removeClass("open").addClass("closed").hide();
			// UPDATE THE SEARCH WINDOW
			$("#gb-search-window").removeClass("hidden").text(jQuery.trim($(this).text()));
			$(".gb-search-form").addClass("hidden");
			// UPDATE THE SEARCH TYPE
			$("#gb-search-type").text("link");
			$("#gb-search-link").text($(this).attr("href"));
		});
		
		// SEARCH CLICK
		$("#gb-search-shortcuts li.search").click(function(e) {
			e.preventDefault();
			// CLOSE EVERYTHING UP
			$(".gb-search-btn.dropdown").removeClass("open").addClass("closed")
			$("#gb-search-shortcuts").removeClass("open").addClass("closed").hide();
			// UPDATE THE SEARCH WINDOW
			$("#gb-search-window").addClass("hidden").empty();
			$(".gb-search-form").removeClass("hidden");
			$("#gb-search .gb-search-input").focus();
			// UPDATE THE SEARCH TYPE
			$("#gb-search-type").text("search");
			$("#gb-search-link").text("empty");
		});
		*/
			$("#gb-search-window").addClass("hidden").empty();
			$(".gb-search-form").removeClass("hidden");
			$("#gb-search .gb-search-input").focus();
			$("#gb-search-type").text("search");
			$("#gb-search-link").text("empty");
	
		// SUBMIT SEARCH
		$(".gb-search-btn.search").click(function() {
			if(jQuery.trim($("#gb-search-type").text()) != "empty") {
				// SUBMIT THE SEARCH FORM
				if(jQuery.trim($("#gb-search-type").text()) == "search") {
					window.location.href = "/site/Default.aspx?PageType=6&SiteID=4&SearchString=" + $("#gb-search .gb-search-input").val();
				}
				
				// FOLLOW LINK URL
				else if(jQuery.trim($("#gb-search-type").text()) == "link") {
					window.location.href = jQuery.trim($("#gb-search-link").text());
				}
			}
		});
		
		// SEARCH FORM SUBMIT
		$(".gb-search-form").submit(function(e){
		    e.preventDefault();
		    window.location.href = "/site/Default.aspx?PageType=6&SiteID=4&SearchString=" + $("#gb-search .gb-search-input").val();
		});
		
		
		// SEARCH INPUT VALUE
		$(".gb-search-input, .gb-channel-search-input").focus(function() {
		    if($(this).val() == "Search this site...") {
		        $(this).val("");
		    }
		});
		$(".gb-search-input, .gb-channel-search-input").blur(function() {
		    if($(this).val() == "") {
		        $(this).val("Search this site...");
		    }
		});
		
		// CHANNEL SEARCH
		$("#gb-channel-search").click(function() {
			if($(this).hasClass("closed")) {
				$(".gb-channel-search-form").slideDown(function() {
					$("#gb-channel-search").removeClass("closed").addClass("open");
				});
			} else {
				$(".gb-channel-search-form").slideUp(function() {
					$("#gb-channel-search").removeClass("open").addClass("closed");
				});
			}
		});
		$(".gb-channel-search-input").click(function() {
			return false;
		});
		
		// SEARCH FORM SUBMIT
		$(".gb-channel-search-form").submit(function(e){
		    	e.preventDefault();
		    	window.location.href = "/site/Default.aspx?PageType=6&SiteID=4&SearchString=" + $("#gb-channel-search .gb-channel-search-input").val();
		});
		$(".gb-channel-search-submit").click(function() {
			$(".gb-channel-search-form").submit();
		});
	}
	
	function calendarListView(){
		//DOC auto click function for schoolwires calendar list view for small mobile devices
		if(!$(".ui-widget.app.calendar #calendarlist-pnl-specialview.loaded").length){
			$("a.ui-btn-toggle.list").click();
			$("a.ui-btn-toggle.month").click();
			$(".ui-widget.app.calendar #calendarlist-pnl-specialview").addClass("loaded");
		}
		
		var getWidth = jsBreakPoint();
		if(getWidth >= 640){ // 640+
			$(".ui-widget.app.calendar #calendar").removeClass("ui-helper-hidden");
			$(".ui-widget.app.calendar #calendarlist-pnl-specialview").addClass("ui-helper-hidden");
		} if(getWidth < 640){ // 480-
			$(".ui-widget.app.calendar #calendar").addClass("ui-helper-hidden");
			$(".ui-widget.app.calendar #calendarlist-pnl-specialview").removeClass("ui-helper-hidden");
			$(".ui-btn-toggle.month").removeClass("active");
			$(".ui-btn-toggle.list").addClass("active");
		}
	}
	
	function headlineScroller() {
		if($(".hp").length) {
			var getWidth = jsBreakPoint();
			$(".ui-widget.app.headlines").each(function() {
				var element = $(this);
				
				// ADD SCROLL ARROWS AND ADD CLASSES
				$(element).prepend("<div class='headlines-scroll-ctrl back icon-font hidden'>Q</div>").append("<div class='headlines-scroll-ctrl next icon-font hidden'>R</div>");
				$(".ui-articles li", element).last().addClass("last");
				
				// SET WIDTH OF HEADLINES
				var headlineNum = $(".ui-articles li", element).length;
				var headlineWidth = 0;
				if (getWidth == 960) { // 960
					headlineWidth = $(".ui-widget-detail", element).width() / 4;
				} if (getWidth == 768 || getWidth == 640 || getWidth == 480) { // 768, 640, 480
					headlineWidth = $(".ui-widget-detail", element).width() / 2;
				} if (getWidth == 320) { // 320
					headlineWidth = $(".ui-widget-detail", element).width();
				}
				$(".ui-articles li", element).each(function() {
					$(this).css("width", headlineWidth + "px");
					
					// ADD RECORD TYPE CLASS WHILE WE ARE HERE
					$(this).addClass("cs-" + jQuery.trim($(".img img", this).attr("alt")));
				});
				
				$(".ui-articles", element).css("width", (headlineWidth * headlineNum));
				
				// SHOW ARROWS IF NEEDED
				if($(".ui-articles", element).width() > $(".ui-widget-detail", element).width()){
					$(".headlines-scroll-ctrl", element).removeClass("hidden");
				}
				
				// MOVE THE MORE LINK
				$(".more-link", element).text("SEE ALL NEWS & VIDEOS").insertBefore($(".ui-widget-footer", element));
				//$(element).append($(".more-link", element));
				
				// SCROLL FUNCTION
				$(".headlines-scroll-ctrl", element).click(function() {
					// GET SCROLL DIMENSIONS
					var scrollDistance = $(".ui-articles li", element).outerWidth(true);
					//var firstScrollDistance = $(".ui-articles li", element).first().outerWidth(true);
					//var lastScrollDistance = $(".ui-articles li", element).last().outerWidth(true);
					var slidePos = parseInt($(".ui-articles", element).css("margin-left")) * -1;
					var overflowDistance = parseInt($(".ui-articles", element).css("width")) - $(".ui-widget-detail", element).width();
					var lastScroll = overflowDistance - slidePos;
					var newPos = 0;
					
					// ANIMATE THE THUMBNAIL SLIDE
					if($(this).hasClass("next")) {
					    if(lastScroll < scrollDistance) {
					        newPos = slidePos + lastScroll;
					    } else {
					        newPos = slidePos + scrollDistance;
					    }    
					
					    $(".ui-articles", element).animate({
					        marginLeft: "-" + newPos + "px"
					    }, 400);
					} else if($(this).hasClass("back")) {
					    if(slidePos < scrollDistance) {
					        newPos = 0;
					    } else {
					        newPos = slidePos - scrollDistance;   
					    }
					
					    $(".ui-articles", element).animate({
					        marginLeft: "-" + newPos + "px"
					    }, 400);
					}	
				});
			});
		}
		
	}
	
	function headlineScrollerResize() {
		if($(".hp").length) {
			var getWidth = jsBreakPoint();
			$(".ui-widget.app.headlines").each(function() {
				var element = $(this);
				$(".ui-articles", element).css("margin-left","0");
				
				// SET WIDTH OF HEADLINES
				var headlineNum = $(".ui-articles li", element).length;
				var headlineWidth = 0;
				if (getWidth == 960) { // 960
					headlineWidth = $(".ui-widget-detail", element).width() / 4;
				} if (getWidth == 768 || getWidth == 640 || getWidth == 480) { // 768, 640, 480
					headlineWidth = $(".ui-widget-detail", element).width() / 2;
				} if (getWidth == 320) { // 320
					headlineWidth = $(".ui-widget-detail", element).width()
				}
				$(".ui-articles li", element).each(function() {
					$(this).css("width", headlineWidth + "px");
				});
				
				$(".ui-articles", element).css("width", (headlineWidth * headlineNum));
				
				// SHOW ARROWS IF NEEDED
				if($(".ui-articles", element).width() > $(".ui-widget-detail", element).width()){
					$(".headlines-scroll-ctrl", element).removeClass("hidden");
				}
			});
		}
	}
	
	function jsBreakPoint(){
		// 960
		if ($(window).width() >= 1024) { return 960; } 
				
		// 768
		if ($(window).width() >= 768 && $(window).width() < 1024) { return 768; }
				
		// 640
		if ($(window).width() >= 640 && $(window).width() < 768) { return 640; }
				
		// 480
		if ($(window).width() >= 480 && $(window).width() < 640) { return 480; }
				
		// 320
		if ($(window).width() >= 320 && $(window).width() < 480) { return 320; }
	}
	
	function homepageWatermarks() {
		var watermarkImgs = [
			["false", "/cms/lib/WA01919505/Centricity/Template/GlobalAssets/images///SSD_template/20150421_watermark_b01_85.png"],
			["false", "/cms/lib/WA01919505/Centricity/Template/GlobalAssets/images///SSD_template/20150421_watermark_b02_85.png"],
			["false", "/cms/lib/WA01919505/Centricity/Template/GlobalAssets/images///SSD_template/20150421_watermark_b04_85.png"],
			["false", "/cms/lib/WA01919505/Centricity/Template/GlobalAssets/images///SSD_template/pencil-primary-15.png"],
			["false", "/cms/lib/WA01919505/Centricity/Template/GlobalAssets/images///SSD_template/20150421_watermark_b06_85.png"],
			["false", "/cms/lib/WA01919505/Centricity/Template/GlobalAssets/images///SSD_template/20150421_watermark_b07_85.png"],
			["false", "/cms/lib/WA01919505/Centricity/Template/GlobalAssets/images///SSD_template/20150421_watermark_b08_85.png"],
			["false", "/cms/lib/WA01919505/Centricity/Template/GlobalAssets/images///SSD_template/SSD_watermark05.png"]
		];
		
		var watermarkCSS = "<style type='text/css'>", haveImgs = 0, contNum = 5;
		for (var i in watermarkImgs) {
			if(watermarkImgs[i][0] == "true") {
				var imgSrc = jQuery.trim(watermarkImgs[i][1]);
				var srcSplit = imgSrc.split("/");
				var srcSplitLen = srcSplit.length;
				if(imgSrc != "" && srcSplit[srcSplitLen - 1] != "default-man.jpg") {
					watermarkCSS +=	".hp-content-region-outer.container" + contNum + " .hp-content-region {" +
								"background: url(" + imgSrc + ") no-repeat left bottom;" +
							"}";
					haveImgs = 1;
				}
			}
			
			contNum++;
		}
		watermarkCSS += "</style>";
		
		if(haveImgs) {
			$("#gb-page").prepend(watermarkCSS);
		}
		
		// fix for EXPLORE ICONS (The megaphones for LMS and SMS)
		var siteAlias = "sumnersd";
		if(siteAlias == "sms" || siteAlias == "lms"){
		      $('#hp-region-container10 span.icon-font').css("font-size", "26px");
		}
	}

				// BUILD LINKS
				var megaLinks = "<div class='mega-channel-links-column ui-clear'>", megaLinksCheck = 0, megaLinkNum = 0;

						megaLinkNum++;
					}
				}
				megaLinks += "</div>";
				if(megaLinksCheck == 1) {
					megaData += "<div class='mega-column one'>" + megaLinks + "</div>";
				}
				
				// ADD TITLE AND CAPTION
				megaData += "<div class='mega-column two'><h1 class='mega-channel-title'>" + $("> a span", this).text() + "</h1><p class='mega-channel-caption'>" + jQuery.trim(megaMenuData[i][0][1]) + "</p></div>";
				
				$(".sw-channel-dropdown.outer .mega-columns", this).prepend(megaData);
				
				// ADD IMAGE
				var imgSrc = jQuery.trim(megaMenuData[i][0][0]);
				var srcSplit = imgSrc.split("/");
				var srcSplitLen = srcSplit.length;
				if(imgSrc != "" && srcSplit[srcSplitLen - 1] != "default-man.jpg") {
					$(".sw-channel-dropdown.outer .mega-columns", this).append("<div class='mega-column four'><div class='mega-channel-bg-img'><img src='" + imgSrc + "' /></div></div>");
				}
			}
		});
	}

								'<a href="http://sumnersd.org/dee">Donald Eismann Elementary</a>' +
							'</li>' +
							'<li>' +
								'<a href="http://sumnersd.org/ehe">Emerald Hills Elementary</a>' +
							'</li>' +
							'<li>' +
								'<a href="http://sumnersd.org/lre">Liberty Ridge Elementary</a>' +
							'</li>' +
							'<li>' +
								'<a href="http://sumnersd.org/mle">Maple Lawn Elementary</a>' +
							'</li>' +
							'<li>' +
								'<a href="http://sumnersd.org/vfe">Victor Falls Elementary</a>' +
							'</li>' +
						'</ul>' +
					'</div>';
		var pageHost = window.location.host;
		if(pageHost != "translate.googleusercontent.com") {				
			$(".gb-global-icon.first").append(schoolDropdown);
			$(".gb-global-icon.first").click(function() {
				$(".gb-mystart-list", this).toggle();
			});
		}
		
	}	

	function addFramesetTranslate() {
		var pageURL = window.location.href;
		var translateDropdown = '<div class="gb-mystart-list">' +
						'<ul>' +
							'<li>' +
								'<a href="http://translate.google.com/translate?u=' + pageURL + '&langpair=en|es&hl=en&anno=0&ie=UTF8">English to Spanish</a>' +
							'</li>' +
							'<li>' +
								'<a href="http://translate.google.com/translate?u=' + pageURL + '&langpair=en|ar&hl=en&anno=0&ie=UTF8">English to Arabic</a>' +
							'</li>' +
							'<li>' +
								'<a href="http://translate.google.com/translate?u=' + pageURL + '&langpair=en|zh-CN&hl=en&anno=0&ie=UTF8">English to Chinese (Simplified)</a>' +
							'</li>' +
							'<li>' +
								'<a href="http://translate.google.com/translate?u=' + pageURL + '&langpair=en|zh-TW&hl=en&anno=0&ie=UTF8">English to Chinese (Traditional)</a>' +
							'</li>' +
							'<li>' +
								'<a href="http://translate.google.com/translate?u=' + pageURL + '&langpair=en|fr&hl=en&anno=0&ie=UTF8">English to French</a>' +
							'</li>' +
							'<li>' +
								'<a href="http://translate.google.com/translate?u=' + pageURL + '&langpair=en|de&hl=en&anno=0&ie=UTF8">English to German</a>' +
							'</li>' +
							'<li>' +
								'<a href="http://translate.google.com/translate?u=' + pageURL + '&langpair=en|it&hl=en&anno=0&ie=UTF8">English to Italian</a>' +
							'</li>' +
							'<li>' +
								'<a href="http://translate.google.com/translate?u=' + pageURL + '&langpair=en|ja&hl=en&anno=0&ie=UTF8">English to Japanese</a>' +
							'</li>' +
							'<li>' +
								'<a href="http://translate.google.com/translate?u=' + pageURL + '&langpair=en|ko&hl=en&anno=0&ie=UTF8">English to Korean</a>' +
							'</li>' +
							'<li>' +
								'<a href="http://translate.google.com/translate?u=' + pageURL + '&langpair=en|pt&hl=en&anno=0&ie=UTF8">English to Portuguese</a>' +
							'</li>' +
							'<li>' +
								'<a href="http://translate.google.com/translate?u=' + pageURL + '&langpair=en|ru&hl=en&anno=0&ie=UTF8">English to Russian</a>' +
							'</li>' +
						'</ul>' +
					'</div>';
		var pageHost = window.location.host;
		if(pageHost != "translate.googleusercontent.com") {				
			$(".gb-global-icon.translate").append(translateDropdown);
			$(".gb-global-icon.translate").click(function() {
				$(".gb-mystart-list", this).toggle();
			});
		}
		
	}

<script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function() {
        channelHoverIE();
        channelTouch();
        closeMenuByPressingKey();
    });

    function channelTouch() {
        // this will change the dropdown behavior when it is touched vs clicked.
        // channels will be clickable on second click. first click simply opens the menu.
        $('#channel-navigation > .sw-channel-item > a').on({
            'touchstart': function (e) {
                
                // see if has menu
                if ($(this).siblings('ul.sw-channel-dropdown li').length > 0) {
                    var button = $(this);

                    // add href as property if not already set
                    // then remove href attribute
                    if (!button.prop('linkHref')) {
                        button.prop('linkHref', button.attr('href'));
                        button.removeAttr('href');
                    }

                    // check to see if menu is already open
                    if ($(this).siblings('ul.sw-channel-dropdown').is(':visible')) {
                        // if open go to link
                        window.location.href = button.prop('linkHref');
                    } 

                } 
            }
        });
    }


    
    function channelHoverIE(){
		// set z-index for IE7
		var parentZindex = $('#channel-navigation').parents('div:first').css('z-index');
		var zindex = (parentZindex > 0 ? parentZindex : 8000);
		$(".sw-channel-item").each(function(ind) {
			$(this).css('z-index', zindex - ind);
			zindex --;
		});
	    $(".sw-channel-item").hover(function(){
	        var subList = $(this).children('ul');
	        if ($.trim(subList.html()) !== "") {
	            subList.show();
	            subList.attr("aria-hidden", "false").attr("aria-expanded", "true");
		    }
		    $(this).addClass("hover");
	    }, function() {
	        $(".sw-channel-dropdown").hide();
	        $(this).removeClass("hover");
	        var subList = $(this).children('ul');
	        if ($.trim(subList.html()) !== "") {
	            subList.attr("aria-hidden", "true").attr("aria-expanded", "false");
	        }
	    });
    }

    function closeMenuByPressingKey() {
        $(".sw-channel-item").each(function(ind) {
            $(this).keyup(function (event) {
                if (event.keyCode == 27) { // ESC
                    $(".sw-channel-dropdown").hide();
                    $(this).removeClass("hover");
                    var subList = $(this).children('ul');
                    if ($.trim(subList.html()) !== "") {
                        subList.attr("aria-hidden", "true").attr("aria-expanded", "false");
                    }
                }
                if (event.keyCode == 13 || event.keyCode == 32) { //enter or space
                    $(this).find('a').get(0).click();
                }
            }); 
        });

        $(".sw-channel-item a").each(function (ind) {
            $(this).parents('.sw-channel-item').keydown(function (e) {
                if (e.keyCode == 9) { // TAB
                    $(".sw-channel-dropdown").hide();
                    $(this).removeClass("hover");
                    var subList = $(this).children('ul');
                    if ($.trim(subList.html()) !== "") {
                        subList.attr("aria-hidden", "true").attr("aria-expanded", "false");
                    }
                }
            });
        });

        $(".sw-channel-dropdown li").each(function(ind) {
            $(this).keydown(function (event) {
                if (event.keyCode == 9) { // TAB
                    $(".sw-channel-dropdown").hide();
                    var parentMenuItem = $(this).parent().closest('li');
                    parentMenuItem.removeClass("hover");
                    var subList = parentMenuItem.children('ul');
                    if ($.trim(subList.html()) !== "") {
                        subList.attr("aria-hidden", "true").attr("aria-expanded", "false");
                    }
                    parentMenuItem.next().find('a:first').focus();
                    event.preventDefault();
                    event.stopPropagation();
                }

                if (event.keyCode == 37 || // left arrow
                    event.keyCode == 39) { // right arrow
                    $(".sw-channel-dropdown").hide();
                    var parentMenuItem = $(this).parent().closest('li');
                    parentMenuItem.removeClass("hover");
                    var subList = parentMenuItem.children('ul');
                    if ($.trim(subList.html()) !== "") {
                        subList.attr("aria-hidden", "true").attr("aria-expanded", "false");
                    }
                    if (event.keyCode == 37) {
                        parentMenuItem.prev().find('a:first').focus();
                    } else {
                        parentMenuItem.next().find('a:first').focus();
                    }
                    event.preventDefault();
                    event.stopPropagation();
                }
            });
        });
    }

</script>


					</div>
					<div id="gb-channel-search" class="hide960 show640 closed">

							<span class="icon-font">V</span>

								<input type="text" class="gb-channel-search-input" value="Search this site..." />
								<div class="gb-channel-search-submit">GO</div>
							</form>
						</div>
